         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         def load_destinations():
             filepath = 'data/destinations.txt'
             destinations = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return destinations
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         dest_id = int(parts[0])
                         name = parts[1]
                         country = parts[2]
                         region = parts[3]
                         description = parts[4]
                         attractions = [a.strip() for a in parts[5].split(',')] if parts[5].strip() else []
                         climate = parts[6]
                         destinations.append({
                             'dest_id': dest_id,
                             'name': name,
                             'country': country,
                             'region': region,
                             'description': description,
                             'attractions': attractions,
                             'climate': climate
                         })
             except Exception:
                 # on any file I/O error, return empty list
                 return []
             return destinations
         
         def load_featured_destinations():
             # For dashboard featured_destinations - can use first 3 destinations if available with only needed fields
             destinations = load_destinations()
             featured = []
             for d in destinations[:3]:
                 featured.append({
                     'dest_id': d['dest_id'],
                     'name': d['name'],
                     'country': d['country'],
                     'image_url': f"/static/images/destinations/{d['dest_id']}.jpg"
                 })
             return featured
         
         def load_upcoming_trips():
             filepath = 'data/trips.txt'
             trips = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return trips
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         trip_id = int(parts[0])
                         trip_name = parts[1]
                         # destination = parts[2]  # not needed here
                         start_date = parts[3]
                         end_date = parts[4]
                         # total_budget = parts[5] # not needed here
                         # status = parts[6]       # not needed here
                         # created_date = parts[7] # not needed here
                         # We consider all trips as upcoming for dashboard
                         trips.append({
                             'trip_id': trip_id,
                             'trip_name': trip_name,
                             'start_date': start_date,
                             'end_date': end_date
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return trips
         
         def load_regions():
             # Fixed regions list from specification
             return ['Asia', 'Europe', 'Americas', 'Africa', 'Oceania']
         
         def load_destinations_minimal():
             # load destinations with subset of fields for destinations page

             destinations_all = load_destinations()

                     'country': d['country'],
                     'region': d['region'],
                     'image_url': f"/static/images/destinations/{d['dest_id']}.jpg"
                 })
             return result

         def load_hotels():
             filepath = 'data/hotels.txt'
             hotels = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return hotels
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         hotel_id = int(parts[0])
                         name = parts[1]
                         city = parts[2]
                         try:
                             rating = float(parts[3])
                         except ValueError:
                             rating = 0.0
                         try:
                             price_per_night = float(parts[4])
                         except ValueError:
                             price_per_night = 0.0
                         amenities = [a.strip() for a in parts[5].split(',')] if parts[5].strip() else []
                         category = parts[6]
                         hotels.append({
                             'hotel_id': hotel_id,
                             'name': name,

                             'rating': rating,
                             'price_per_night': price_per_night,
                             'amenities': amenities,
                             'category': category
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return hotels
         
         def load_flights():
             filepath = 'data/flights.txt'
             flights = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return flights
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 9:
                             continue
                         flight_id = int(parts[0])
                         airline = parts[1]
                         departure_city = parts[2]
                         arrival_city = parts[3]
                         departure_time = parts[4]
                         arrival_time = parts[5]
                         try:
                             price = float(parts[6])
                         except ValueError:
                             price = 0.0
                         class_type = parts[7]
                         duration = parts[8]
                         flights.append({
                             'flight_id': flight_id,
                             'airline': airline,
                             'departure_city': departure_city,
                             'arrival_city': arrival_city,
                             'departure_time': departure_time,
                             'arrival_time': arrival_time,
                             'price': price,
                             'class_type': class_type,
                             'duration': duration
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return flights
         
         def load_packages():
             filepath = 'data/packages.txt'
             packages = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return packages
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         package_id = int(parts[0])
                         package_name = parts[1]
                         destination = parts[2]
                         try:
                             duration_days = int(parts[3])
                         except ValueError:
                             duration_days = 0
                         try:

                         except ValueError:
                             price = 0.0

             except Exception:
                 return []

         def load_trips():
             filepath = 'data/trips.txt'
             trips = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return trips
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         trip_id = int(parts[0])
                         trip_name = parts[1]
                         destination = parts[2]
                         start_date = parts[3]
                         end_date = parts[4]
                         try:
                             total_budget = float(parts[5])
                         except ValueError:
                             total_budget = 0.0
                         status = parts[6]
                         created_date = parts[7]
                         trips.append({
                             'trip_id': trip_id,
                             'trip_name': trip_name,
                             'destination': destination,
                             'start_date': start_date,
                             'end_date': end_date,
                             'total_budget': total_budget,
                             'status': status,
                             'created_date': created_date
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return trips
         
         def load_booking(booking_id):
             filepath = 'data/bookings.txt'
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return None
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         b_id = int(parts[0])
                         if b_id == booking_id:
                             trip_id = int(parts[1])
                             booking_type = parts[2]
                             booking_date = parts[3]
                             try:
                                 amount = float(parts[4])
                             except ValueError:
                                 amount = 0.0
                             confirmation_number = parts[5]
                             status = parts[6]
                             return {
                                 'booking_id': b_id,
                                 'trip_id': trip_id,
                                 'booking_type': booking_type,
                                 'booking_date': booking_date,
                                 'amount': amount,
                                 'confirmation_number': confirmation_number,
                                 'status': status
                             }
             except Exception:
                 return None
             return None
         
         @app.route('/', methods=['GET'])
         def dashboard_page():
             # Redirect to the dashboard page route is '/' according to spec but needs to render dashboard.html
             # Spec says / route is GET and function dashboard_page, so render dashboard.html with context
             featured_destinations = load_featured_destinations()
             upcoming_trips = load_upcoming_trips()
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_destinations=featured_destinations, upcoming_trips=upcoming_trips)
         
         @app.route('/destinations', methods=['GET'])
         def destinations_page():
             destinations = load_destinations_minimal()
             regions = load_regions()
             return render_template('destinations.html', destinations=destinations, regions=regions)
         
         @app.route('/destination/<int:dest_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def destination_details_page(dest_id):
             destinations = load_destinations()
             destination = None
             for d in destinations:
                 if d['dest_id'] == dest_id:
                     destination = d
                     break
             if not destination:
                 # Destination not found, can return 404 or redirect to destinations page
                 return redirect(url_for('destinations_page'))
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Adding to trip itinerary or redirecting as per functional design
                 # Spec is not explicit about data handling for add-to-trip-button, so here just redirect to itinerary page
                 return redirect(url_for('itinerary_page'))
         
             return render_template('destination_details.html', destination=destination)
         
         @app.route('/itinerary', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def itinerary_page():
             itineraries = load_itineraries()
             regions = load_regions()
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Post triggered by add-activity-button
                 # Spec does not specify actual modification of data files or data persistence, so just reload page
                 # For a real app, code to update/save activities would be here
                 return redirect(url_for('itinerary_page'))
             return render_template('itinerary.html', itineraries=itineraries, regions=regions)
         
         @app.route('/accommodations', methods=['GET'])
         def accommodations_page():
             hotels = load_hotels()
             return render_template('accommodations.html', hotels=hotels)
         
         @app.route('/transportation', methods=['GET'])
         def transportation_page():
             flights = load_flights()
             return render_template('transportation.html', flights=flights)
         
         @app.route('/packages', methods=['GET'])
         def packages_page():
             packages = load_packages()
             durations = ['3-5 days', '7-10 days', '14+ days']
             return render_template('packages.html', packages=packages, durations=durations)
         
         @app.route('/trips', methods=['GET'])
         def trips_page():
             trips = load_trips()
             return render_template('trips.html', trips=trips)
         
         @app.route('/booking-confirmation/<int:booking_id>', methods=['GET'])
         def booking_confirmation_page(booking_id):
             booking = load_booking(booking_id)
             if booking is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             return render_template('booking_confirmation.html', booking=booking)
         
         @app.route('/recommendations', methods=['GET'])
         def recommendations_page():
             # Recommendations data is assumed similar structure as destinations or trips?
             # Spec says recommendations have context variables recommendations (list of dict) and trending_destinations (list of dict)
             # We do not have a file for recommendations; use empty list for recommendations
             recommendations = []
             # For trending_destinations can use destinations with fake popularity or hardcode
             trending_destinations = []
             # Load destinations to build trending_destinations with popularity
             destinations = load_destinations()
             # Assign dummy popularity as length of attractions (just for sample), since no popularity in data files
             for d in destinations:
                 trending_destinations.append({
                     'dest_id': d['dest_id'],
                     'name': d['name'],
                     'popularity': len(d['attractions'])
                 })
             return render_template('recommendations.html', recommendations=recommendations, trending_destinations=trending_destinations)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         # Data loading functions
         
         def load_destinations():
             filepath = 'data/destinations.txt'
             destinations = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return destinations
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line = line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         dest_id = int(parts[0])
                         name = parts[1]
                         country = parts[2]
                         region = parts[3]
                         description = parts[4]
                         attractions = [x.strip() for x in parts[5].split(',')] if parts[5].strip() else []
                         climate = parts[6]
                         destinations.append({
                             'dest_id': dest_id,
                             'name': name,
                             'country': country,
                             'region': region,
                             'description': description,
                             'attractions': attractions,
                             'climate': climate
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return destinations
         
         def load_featured_destinations():
             all_dest = load_destinations()
             featured = []
             for d in all_dest[:3]:
                 featured.append({
                     'dest_id': d['dest_id'],
                     'name': d['name'],
                     'country': d['country'],
                     'image_url': f'/static/images/destinations/{d['dest_id']}.jpg'
                 })
             return featured
         
         def load_upcoming_trips():
             filepath = 'data/trips.txt'
             trips = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return trips
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         trip_id = int(parts[0])
                         trip_name = parts[1]
                         start_date = parts[3]
                         end_date = parts[4]
                         trips.append({
                             'trip_id': trip_id,
                             'trip_name': trip_name,
                             'start_date': start_date,
                             'end_date': end_date
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return trips
         
         def load_regions():
             return ['Asia', 'Europe', 'Americas', 'Africa', 'Oceania']
         
         def load_destinations_for_destinations_page():
             all_dest = load_destinations()
             result = []
             for d in all_dest:
                 result.append({
                     'dest_id': d['dest_id'],
                     'name': d['name'],
                     'country': d['country'],
                     'region': d['region'],
                     'image_url': f'/static/images/destinations/{d['dest_id']}.jpg'
                 })
             return result
         
         def load_itineraries():
             filepath = 'data/itineraries.txt'
             itineraries = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return itineraries
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         itinerary_id = int(parts[0])
                         itinerary_name = parts[1]
                         destination = parts[2]
                         start_date = parts[3]
                         end_date = parts[4]
                         activities = [x.strip() for x in parts[5].split(',')] if parts[5].strip() else []
                         status = parts[6]
                         itineraries.append({
                             'itinerary_id': itinerary_id,
                             'itinerary_name': itinerary_name,
                             'destination': destination,
                             'start_date': start_date,
                             'end_date': end_date,
                             'activities': activities,
                             'status': status
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return itineraries
         
         def load_hotels():
             filepath = 'data/hotels.txt'
             hotels = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return hotels
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         hotel_id = int(parts[0])
                         name = parts[1]
                         city = parts[2]
                         try:
                             rating = float(parts[3])
                         except:
                             rating = 0.0
                         try:
                             price_per_night = float(parts[4])
                         except:
                             price_per_night = 0.0
                         amenities = [x.strip() for x in parts[5].split(',')] if parts[5].strip() else []
                         category = parts[6]
                         hotels.append({
                             'hotel_id': hotel_id,
                             'name': name,
                             'city': city,
                             'rating': rating,
                             'price_per_night': price_per_night,
                             'amenities': amenities,
                             'category': category
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return hotels
         
         def load_flights():
             filepath = 'data/flights.txt'
             flights = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return flights
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 9:
                             continue
                         flight_id = int(parts[0])
                         airline = parts[1]
                         departure_city = parts[2]
                         arrival_city = parts[3]
                         departure_time = parts[4]
                         arrival_time = parts[5]
                         try:
                             price = float(parts[6])
                         except:
                             price = 0.0
                         class_type = parts[7]
                         duration = parts[8]
                         flights.append({
                             'flight_id': flight_id,
                             'airline': airline,
                             'departure_city': departure_city,
                             'arrival_city': arrival_city,
                             'departure_time': departure_time,
                             'arrival_time': arrival_time,
                             'price': price,
                             'class_type': class_type,
                             'duration': duration
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return flights
         
         def load_packages():
             filepath = 'data/packages.txt'
             packages = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return packages
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         package_id = int(parts[0])
                         package_name = parts[1]
                         destination = parts[2]
                         try:
                             duration_days = int(parts[3])
                         except:
                             duration_days = 0
                         try:
                             price = float(parts[4])
                         except:
                             price = 0.0
                         included_items = [x.strip() for x in parts[5].split(',')] if parts[5].strip() else []
                         difficulty_level = parts[6]
                         packages.append({
                             'package_id': package_id,
                             'package_name': package_name,
                             'destination': destination,

                             'price': price,
                             'included_items': included_items,
                             'difficulty_level': difficulty_level
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return packages
         
         def load_trips():
             filepath = 'data/trips.txt'
             trips = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return trips
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         trip_id = int(parts[0])
                         trip_name = parts[1]
                         destination = parts[2]
                         start_date = parts[3]
                         end_date = parts[4]
                         try:
                             total_budget = float(parts[5])
                         except:
                             total_budget = 0.0
                         status = parts[6]
                         created_date = parts[7]
                         trips.append({
                             'trip_id': trip_id,
                             'trip_name': trip_name,
                             'destination': destination,
                             'start_date': start_date,
                             'end_date': end_date,
                             'total_budget': total_budget,
                             'status': status,
                             'created_date': created_date
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return trips
         
         def load_booking(booking_id):
             filepath = 'data/bookings.txt'
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return None
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         b_id = int(parts[0])
                         if b_id == booking_id:
                             trip_id = int(parts[1])
                             booking_type = parts[2]
                             booking_date = parts[3]
                             try:
                                 amount = float(parts[4])
                             except:
                                 amount = 0.0
                             confirmation_number = parts[5]
                             status = parts[6]
                             return {
                                 'booking_id': b_id,
                                 'trip_id': trip_id,
                                 'booking_type': booking_type,
                                 'booking_date': booking_date,
                                 'amount': amount,
                                 'confirmation_number': confirmation_number,
                                 'status': status
                             }
             except Exception:
                 return None
             return None
         
         # Routes
         
         @app.route('/', methods=['GET'])
         def dashboard_page():
             featured_destinations = load_featured_destinations()
             upcoming_trips = load_upcoming_trips()
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_destinations=featured_destinations, upcoming_trips=upcoming_trips)
         
         @app.route('/destinations', methods=['GET'])
         def destinations_page():
             destinations = load_destinations_for_destinations_page()
             regions = load_regions()
             return render_template('destinations.html', destinations=destinations, regions=regions)
         
         @app.route('/destination/<int:dest_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def destination_details_page(dest_id):
             destinations = load_destinations()
             destination = next((d for d in destinations if d['dest_id'] == dest_id), None)
             if destination is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('destinations_page'))
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Functional design says POST stays on this page or redirects to itinerary page
                 return redirect(url_for('itinerary_page'))
             return render_template('destination_details.html', destination=destination)
         
         @app.route('/itinerary', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def itinerary_page():
             itineraries = load_itineraries()
             regions = load_regions()
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Add-activity-button triggers POST, no data persistence specified; simply reload page
                 return redirect(url_for('itinerary_page'))
             return render_template('itinerary.html', itineraries=itineraries, regions=regions)
         
         @app.route('/accommodations', methods=['GET'])
         def accommodations_page():
             hotels = load_hotels()
             return render_template('accommodations.html', hotels=hotels)
         
         @app.route('/transportation', methods=['GET'])
         def transportation_page():
             flights = load_flights()
             return render_template('transportation.html', flights=flights)
         
         @app.route('/packages', methods=['GET'])
         def packages_page():
             packages = load_packages()
             durations = ['3-5 days', '7-10 days', '14+ days']
             return render_template('packages.html', packages=packages, durations=durations)
         
         @app.route('/trips', methods=['GET'])
         def trips_page():
             trips = load_trips()
             return render_template('trips.html', trips=trips)
         
         @app.route('/booking-confirmation/<int:booking_id>', methods=['GET'])
         def booking_confirmation_page(booking_id):
             booking = load_booking(booking_id)
             if booking is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             return render_template('booking_confirmation.html', booking=booking)
         
         @app.route('/recommendations', methods=['GET'])
         def recommendations_page():
             # recommendations data undefined in spec, assume empty
             recommendations = []
             trending_destinations = []
             destinations = load_destinations()
             for d in destinations:
                 trending_destinations.append({
                     'dest_id': d['dest_id'],
                     'name': d['name'],

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         # Data loading functions
         
         def load_destinations():
             filepath = 'data/destinations.txt'
             destinations = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return destinations
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line = line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         dest_id = int(parts[0])
                         name = parts[1]
                         country = parts[2]
                         region = parts[3]
                         description = parts[4]
                         attractions = [x.strip() for x in parts[5].split(',')] if parts[5].strip() else []
                         climate = parts[6]
                         destinations.append({
                             'dest_id': dest_id,
                             'name': name,
                             'country': country,
                             'region': region,
                             'description': description,
                             'attractions': attractions,
                             'climate': climate
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return destinations
         
         def load_featured_destinations():
             all_dest = load_destinations()
             featured = []
             for d in all_dest[:3]:
                 featured.append({
                     'dest_id': d['dest_id'],
                     'name': d['name'],
                     'country': d['country'],
                     'image_url': f"/static/images/destinations/{d['dest_id']}.jpg"
                 })
             return featured
         
         def load_upcoming_trips():
             filepath = 'data/trips.txt'
             trips = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return trips
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         trip_id = int(parts[0])
                         trip_name = parts[1]
                         start_date = parts[3]
                         end_date = parts[4]
                         trips.append({
                             'trip_id': trip_id,
                             'trip_name': trip_name,
                             'start_date': start_date,
                             'end_date': end_date
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return trips
         
         def load_regions():
             return ['Asia', 'Europe', 'Americas', 'Africa', 'Oceania']
         
         def load_destinations_for_destinations_page():
             all_dest = load_destinations()
             result = []
             for d in all_dest:
                 result.append({
                     'dest_id': d['dest_id'],
                     'name': d['name'],
                     'country': d['country'],
                     'region': d['region'],
                     'image_url': f"/static/images/destinations/{d['dest_id']}.jpg"
                 })
             return result
         
         def load_itineraries():
             filepath = 'data/itineraries.txt'
             itineraries = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return itineraries
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         itinerary_id = int(parts[0])
                         itinerary_name = parts[1]
                         destination = parts[2]
                         start_date = parts[3]
                         end_date = parts[4]
                         activities = [x.strip() for x in parts[5].split(',')] if parts[5].strip() else []
                         status = parts[6]
                         itineraries.append({
                             'itinerary_id': itinerary_id,
                             'itinerary_name': itinerary_name,
                             'destination': destination,
                             'start_date': start_date,
                             'end_date': end_date,
                             'activities': activities,
                             'status': status
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return itineraries

                         except:

                         trip_name = parts[1]
                         destination = parts[2]
                         start_date = parts[3]
                         end_date = parts[4]
                         try:
                             total_budget = float(parts[5])
                         except:
                             total_budget = 0.0
                         status = parts[6]
                         created_date = parts[7]
                         trips.append({
                             'trip_id': trip_id,
                             'trip_name': trip_name,
                             'destination': destination,
                             'start_date': start_date,
                             'end_date': end_date,
                             'total_budget': total_budget,
                             'status': status,
                             'created_date': created_date
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return trips
         
         def load_booking(booking_id):
             filepath = 'data/bookings.txt'
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return None
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         b_id = int(parts[0])
                         if b_id == booking_id:
                             trip_id = int(parts[1])
                             booking_type = parts[2]
                             booking_date = parts[3]
                             try:
                                 amount = float(parts[4])
                             except:
                                 amount = 0.0
                             confirmation_number = parts[5]
                             status = parts[6]
                             return {
                                 'booking_id': b_id,
                                 'trip_id': trip_id,
                                 'booking_type': booking_type,
                                 'booking_date': booking_date,
                                 'amount': amount,
                                 'confirmation_number': confirmation_number,
                                 'status': status
                             }
             except Exception:
                 return None
             return None
         
         # Routes
         
         @app.route('/', methods=['GET'])
         def dashboard_page():
             featured_destinations = load_featured_destinations()
             upcoming_trips = load_upcoming_trips()
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_destinations=featured_destinations, upcoming_trips=upcoming_trips)
         
         @app.route('/destinations', methods=['GET'])
         def destinations_page():
             destinations = load_destinations_for_destinations_page()
             regions = load_regions()
             return render_template('destinations.html', destinations=destinations, regions=regions)
         
         @app.route('/destination/<int:dest_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def destination_details_page(dest_id):
             destinations = load_destinations()
             destination = next((d for d in destinations if d['dest_id'] == dest_id), None)
             if destination is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('destinations_page'))
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 return redirect(url_for('itinerary_page'))
             return render_template('destination_details.html', destination=destination)
         
         @app.route('/itinerary', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def itinerary_page():
             itineraries = load_itineraries()
             regions = load_regions()
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 return redirect(url_for('itinerary_page'))
             return render_template('itinerary.html', itineraries=itineraries, regions=regions)
         
         @app.route('/accommodations', methods=['GET'])
         def accommodations_page():
             hotels = load_hotels()
             return render_template('accommodations.html', hotels=hotels)
         
         @app.route('/transportation', methods=['GET'])
         def transportation_page():
             flights = load_flights()
             return render_template('transportation.html', flights=flights)
         
         @app.route('/packages', methods=['GET'])
         def packages_page():
             packages = load_packages()
             durations = ['3-5 days', '7-10 days', '14+ days']
             return render_template('packages.html', packages=packages, durations=durations)
         
         @app.route('/trips', methods=['GET'])
         def trips_page():
             trips = load_trips()
             return render_template('trips.html', trips=trips)
         
         @app.route('/booking-confirmation/<int:booking_id>', methods=['GET'])
         def booking_confirmation_page(booking_id):
             booking = load_booking(booking_id)
             if booking is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             return render_template('booking_confirmation.html', booking=booking)
         
         @app.route('/recommendations', methods=['GET'])
         def recommendations_page():
             recommendations = []
             trending_destinations = []
             destinations = load_destinations()
             for d in destinations:
                 trending_destinations.append({
                     'dest_id': d['dest_id'],
                     'name': d['name'],
                     'popularity': len(d['attractions'])
                 })
             return render_template('recommendations.html', recommendations=recommendations, trending_destinations=trending_destinations)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         def load_destinations():
             filepath = 'data/destinations.txt'
             destinations = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return destinations
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         dest_id = int(parts[0])
                         name = parts[1]
                         country = parts[2]
                         region = parts[3]
                         description = parts[4]
                         attractions = [a.strip() for a in parts[5].split(',')] if parts[5].strip() else []
                         climate = parts[6]
                         destinations.append({
                             'dest_id': dest_id,
                             'name': name,
                             'country': country,
                             'region': region,
                             'description': description,
                             'attractions': attractions,
                             'climate': climate
                         })
             except Exception:
                 # on any file I/O error, return empty list
                 return []
             return destinations
         
         def load_featured_destinations():
             # For dashboard featured_destinations - can use first 3 destinations if available with only needed fields
             destinations = load_destinations()
             featured = []
             for d in destinations[:3]:
                 featured.append({
                     'dest_id': d['dest_id'],
                     'name': d['name'],
                     'country': d['country'],
                     'image_url': f"/static/images/destinations/{d['dest_id']}.jpg"
                 })
             return featured
         
         def load_upcoming_trips():
             filepath = 'data/trips.txt'
             trips = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return trips
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         trip_id = int(parts[0])
                         trip_name = parts[1]
                         # destination = parts[2]  # not needed here
                         start_date = parts[3]
                         end_date = parts[4]
                         # total_budget = parts[5] # not needed here
                         # status = parts[6]       # not needed here
                         # created_date = parts[7] # not needed here
                         # We consider all trips as upcoming for dashboard
                         trips.append({
                             'trip_id': trip_id,
                             'trip_name': trip_name,
                             'start_date': start_date,
                             'end_date': end_date
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return trips
         
         def load_regions():
             # Fixed regions list from specification

         def load_destinations_minimal():

                     'image_url': f"/static/images/destinations/{d['dest_id']}.jpg"
                 })
             return result
         
         def load_itineraries():
             filepath = 'data/itineraries.txt'
             itineraries = []

                 return itineraries
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()

                 return hotels
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         hotel_id = int(parts[0])
                         name = parts[1]
                         city = parts[2]
                         try:
                             rating = float(parts[3])
                         except ValueError:
                             rating = 0.0
                         try:
                             price_per_night = float(parts[4])
                         except ValueError:
                             price_per_night = 0.0
                         amenities = [a.strip() for a in parts[5].split(',')] if parts[5].strip() else []
                         category = parts[6]
                         hotels.append({
                             'hotel_id': hotel_id,
                             'name': name,
                             'city': city,
                             'rating': rating,
                             'price_per_night': price_per_night,
                             'amenities': amenities,
                             'category': category
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return hotels
         
         def load_flights():
             filepath = 'data/flights.txt'
             flights = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return flights
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 9:
                             continue
                         flight_id = int(parts[0])
                         airline = parts[1]
                         departure_city = parts[2]
                         arrival_city = parts[3]
                         departure_time = parts[4]
                         arrival_time = parts[5]
                         try:
                             price = float(parts[6])
                         except ValueError:
                             price = 0.0
                         class_type = parts[7]
                         duration = parts[8]
                         flights.append({
                             'flight_id': flight_id,
                             'airline': airline,
                             'departure_city': departure_city,
                             'arrival_city': arrival_city,
                             'departure_time': departure_time,
                             'arrival_time': arrival_time,
                             'price': price,
                             'class_type': class_type,
                             'duration': duration
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return flights
         
         def load_packages():
             filepath = 'data/packages.txt'
             packages = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return packages
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         package_id = int(parts[0])
                         package_name = parts[1]
                         destination = parts[2]
                         try:
                             duration_days = int(parts[3])
                         except ValueError:
                             duration_days = 0
                         try:
                             price = float(parts[4])
                         except ValueError:
                             price = 0.0
                         included_items = [i.strip() for i in parts[5].split(',')] if parts[5].strip() else []
                         difficulty_level = parts[6]
                         packages.append({
                             'package_id': package_id,
                             'package_name': package_name,
                             'destination': destination,
                             'duration_days': duration_days,
                             'price': price,
                             'included_items': included_items,
                             'difficulty_level': difficulty_level
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return packages
         
         def load_trips():
             filepath = 'data/trips.txt'
             trips = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return trips
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         trip_id = int(parts[0])
                         trip_name = parts[1]
                         destination = parts[2]
                         start_date = parts[3]
                         end_date = parts[4]
                         try:
                             total_budget = float(parts[5])
                         except ValueError:
                             total_budget = 0.0
                         status = parts[6]
                         created_date = parts[7]
                         trips.append({
                             'trip_id': trip_id,
                             'trip_name': trip_name,
                             'destination': destination,
                             'start_date': start_date,
                             'end_date': end_date,
                             'total_budget': total_budget,
                             'status': status,
                             'created_date': created_date
                         })
             except Exception:
                 return []
             return trips
         
         def load_booking(booking_id):
             filepath = 'data/bookings.txt'
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return None
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         b_id = int(parts[0])
                         if b_id == booking_id:
                             trip_id = int(parts[1])
                             booking_type = parts[2]
                             booking_date = parts[3]
                             try:
                                 amount = float(parts[4])
                             except ValueError:
                                 amount = 0.0
                             confirmation_number = parts[5]
                             status = parts[6]
                             return {
                                 'booking_id': b_id,
                                 'trip_id': trip_id,
                                 'booking_type': booking_type,
                                 'booking_date': booking_date,
                                 'amount': amount,
                                 'confirmation_number': confirmation_number,
                                 'status': status
                             }
             except Exception:
                 return None
             return None
         
         @app.route('/', methods=['GET'])
         def dashboard_page():
             # Redirect to the dashboard page route is '/' according to spec but needs to render dashboard.html
             # Spec says / route is GET and function dashboard_page, so render dashboard.html with context
             featured_destinations = load_featured_destinations()
             upcoming_trips = load_upcoming_trips()
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_destinations=featured_destinations, upcoming_trips=upcoming_trips)
         
         @app.route('/destinations', methods=['GET'])
         def destinations_page():
             destinations = load_destinations_minimal()
             regions = load_regions()
             return render_template('destinations.html', destinations=destinations, regions=regions)
         
         @app.route('/destination/<int:dest_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def destination_details_page(dest_id):
             destinations = load_destinations()
             destination = None
             for d in destinations:
                 if d['dest_id'] == dest_id:
                     destination = d
                     break
             if not destination:
                 # Destination not found, can return 404 or redirect to destinations page
                 return redirect(url_for('destinations_page'))
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Adding to trip itinerary or redirecting as per functional design
                 # Spec is not explicit about data handling for add-to-trip-button, so here just redirect to itinerary page
                 return redirect(url_for('itinerary_page'))
         
             return render_template('destination_details.html', destination=destination)
         
         @app.route('/itinerary', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def itinerary_page():
             itineraries = load_itineraries()
             regions = load_regions()
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Post triggered by add-activity-button
                 # Spec does not specify actual modification of data files or data persistence, so just reload page
                 # For a real app, code to update/save activities would be here
                 return redirect(url_for('itinerary_page'))
             return render_template('itinerary.html', itineraries=itineraries, regions=regions)
         
         @app.route('/accommodations', methods=['GET'])
         def accommodations_page():
             hotels = load_hotels()
             return render_template('accommodations.html', hotels=hotels)
         
         @app.route('/transportation', methods=['GET'])
         def transportation_page():
             flights = load_flights()
             return render_template('transportation.html', flights=flights)
         
         @app.route('/packages', methods=['GET'])
         def packages_page():
             packages = load_packages()
             durations = ['3-5 days', '7-10 days', '14+ days']
             return render_template('packages.html', packages=packages, durations=durations)
         
         @app.route('/trips', methods=['GET'])
         def trips_page():
             trips = load_trips()
             return render_template('trips.html', trips=trips)
         
         @app.route('/booking-confirmation/<int:booking_id>', methods=['GET'])
         def booking_confirmation_page(booking_id):
             booking = load_booking(booking_id)
             if booking is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             return render_template('booking_confirmation.html', booking=booking)
         
         @app.route('/recommendations', methods=['GET'])
         def recommendations_page():
             # Recommendations data is assumed similar structure as destinations or trips?
             # Spec says recommendations have context variables recommendations (list of dict) and trending_destinations (list of dict)
             # We do not have a file for recommendations; use empty list for recommendations
             recommendations = []
             # For trending_destinations can use destinations with fake popularity or hardcode
             trending_destinations = []
             # Load destinations to build trending_destinations with popularity
             destinations = load_destinations()
             # Assign dummy popularity as length of attractions (just for sample), since no popularity in data files
             for d in destinations:
                 trending_destinations.append({
                     'dest_id': d['dest_id'],
                     'name': d['name'],
                     'popularity': len(d['attractions'])
                 })
             return render_template('recommendations.html', recommendations=recommendations, trending_destinations=trending_destinations)

             app.run(debug=True)
